Āmantane-etu <pb ed="M" n="0.0365" /> vessantaro rājā <note>jā. 2.22.2341</note>, ‘‘ehi bhikkhu cara brahmacariyaṃ <note>mahāva. 28</note>, etha bhikkhave sīlavā hotha’’ iccādīsupi ehi, ethasaddā āmantane tiṭṭhanti.

Nimantane-adhivāsetu me bhante bhagavā svātanāya bhattaṃ <note>pārā. 77</note>.

Pavedane-vedayatīti maṃ saṅgho dhāretu <note>cūḷava. aṭṭha. 102</note>, upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu <note>dī. ni. 1.299</note>, punārāyu ca me laddho, evaṃ jānāhi mārisa <note>dī. ni. 2.369</note>.

Pattakāle-parinibbātu bhante bhagavā, parinibbātu sugato, parinibbānakālo bhante bhagavato <note>dī. ni. 2.168</note>, kālo kho te mahāvīra, uppajja mātukucchiyaṃ <note>bu. vaṃ. 1.67</note>, byākarohi aggivessana na dāni te tuṇhībhāvassa kālo <note>ma. ni. 1.357</note>.

Anubhotu, anubhontu, anubhohi, anubhotha, anubhomi, anubhoma, bhavatu, bhavantu, ‘himimesvassā’ti hi, mi, mesu assa dīgho, tvaṃ paṇḍito bhavāhi.

§576. **Hissato lopo** <note>ka. 479; rū. 452; nī. 960; caṃ. 5.3.99; pā. 6.4.105</note>.

Akārato parassa hissa lopo hoti.

Atoti kiṃ? Brūhi, dehi, hohi.

Iminā ato hissa lopo, tvaṃ paṇḍito bhava.

Tumhe paṇḍitā bhavatha, bhavāmi, bhavāma.

Parachakke-so bhavataṃ, te bhavantaṃ, tvaṃ bhavassu, tumhe bhavavho, ahaṃ bhave, mayaṃ bhavāmase, imāni suddhakatturūpāni.

Anubhūyatu<pb ed="M" n="0.0366" />, anubhūyantu, anubhuyyatu, anubhuyyantu iccādi suddhakammarūpaṃ.

Bhāvetu, bhāventu, bhāvayatu, bhāvayantu iccādi hetukatturūpaṃ.

Bhāvīyatu, bhāvīyantu. Rassatte-bhāviyatu, bhāviyantu. Dvitte-bhāviyyatu, bhāviyyantu. Tathā bhāvayīyatu, bhāvayīyantuiccādi hetukammarūpaṃ.

‘Eyyāthasse’iccādisuttena thassa vho, tumhe bhavavho, bhavatha vā.

Iti tvādi.

#### Eyyādi

Atha eyyādi vuccate.

§577. **Hetuphalesveyya eyyuṃ eyyāsi eyyātha eyyāmi eyyāma etha eraṃ etho eyyāvho** <note>eyyavho (moggallānādīsu)</note> **eyyaṃ eyyāmhe vā** <note>ka. 416; rū. 454; nī. 880; caṃ. 1.3.120; pā. 3.3.156</note>.

Aññamaññasambandhiniyā hetukriyāyañca phalakriyāyañca kriyatthā eyyādayo honti vā. Hetuphalesupi kadāci aññavibhattuppattidīpanattho vāsaddo, sace so yānaṃ labhissati, gamissati, sace na labhissati, na gamissati iccādi.

Sace saṅkhāro nicco bhaveyya, sukho nāma bhaveyya, sace so paṇḍito bhaveyya, sukhito bhaveyya.

§578. **Pañhapatthanāvidhīsu** <note>caṃ. 1.3.121; pā. 3.3.161</note>.

Etesu <pb ed="M" n="0.0367" /> eyyādayo honti.

Pañhe-kinnu kho tvaṃ vinayaṃ vā adhiyyeyyāsi dhammaṃ vā.

Patthanāyaṃ-bhaveyyaṃ jātijātiyaṃ.

Vidhimhi-pāṇaṃ na haneyya, adinnaṃ na ādiyeyya, dānaṃ dadeyya, sīlaṃ rakkheyya.

§579. **Sattārahesveyyādī** <note>ka. 416; rū. 454; nī. 881-4; caṃ. 1.3.128; pā. 3.3.169-172; satyarahesveyyādī (bahūsu)</note>.

Sattiyaṃ arahatthe ca eyyādayo honti.

Bhavaṃ rajjaṃ kareyya, bhavaṃ rajjaṃ kātuṃ sakko, kātuṃ arahoti attho.

So imaṃ vijaṭaye jaṭaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.23</note>.

§580. **Sambhāvane vā** <note>ka. 416; rū. 854; nī. 881, 883-4; caṃ. 1.3.118-9; pā. 3.3.154-5</note>.

Sambhāvanepi eyyādayo honti vā.

Pabbatamapi sirasā bhindeyya, bhaveyya, bhaveyyuṃ, bhaveyyāsi, bhaveyyātha, bhaveyyāmi, bhaveyyāma.

Parachakke-so bhavetha, te bhaveraṃ, tvaṃ bhavetho, tumhe bhaveyyāvho, ahaṃ bhaveyyaṃ, mayaṃ bhaveyyāmhe, iti suddhakatturūpāni.

Anubhūyeyya, anubhūyeyyuṃ. Dvitte rassattaṃ, anubhuyyeyya, anubhuyyeyyuṃ iccādi suddhakammarūpaṃ.

Bhāveyya<pb ed="M" n="0.0368" />, bhāveyyuṃ, bhāvayeyya, bhāvayeyyuṃ iccādi hetukatturūpaṃ.

Bhāvīyeyya, bhāvīyeyyuṃ. Rassatte-bhāvayiyeyya, bhāvayiyeyyuṃ. Dvitte-bhāviyyeyya, bhāviyyeyyuṃ. Tathā bhāvayīyeyya, bhāvayīyeyyuṃ iccādi hetukammarūpaṃ.

§581. **Eyyeyyāseyyaṃnaṃ ṭe** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Eyya, eyyāsi, eyyamiccetesaṃ ṭe hoti vā.

Atrimā pāḷī-caje mattā sukhaṃ dhīro, passe ce vipulaṃ sukhaṃ <note>dha. pa. 290</note>. Kiṃ tvaṃ sutasomā’nutappe <note>jā. 2.21.399</note>, dhīraṃ passe suṇe dhīraṃ, dhīrena saha saṃvase <note>jā. 1.13.94</note> iccādi.

So bhave, bhaveyya, tvaṃ bhave, bhaveyyāsi, ahaṃ bhave, bhaveyyaṃ.

§582. **Eyyuṃssuṃ** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Eyyuṃssa uṃ hoti vā.

Atrimā pāḷī-vajjuṃ vā te na vā vajjuṃ, natthi nāsāya rūhanā <note>jā. 1.3.33</note>, upayānāni me dajjuṃ, rājaputta tayī gateti <note>jā. 2.22.26</note>.

§583. **Eyyāmassemu ca** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Eyyāmassa emu ca hoti, antassa u ca.

Atrimā pāḷī-kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ <note>dī. ni. 2.318</note>, muñcemu naṃ uragaṃ bandhanasmā <note>jā. 1.15.252</note>, dakkhemu te nāga nivesanāni <note>jā. 1.15.254</note>, gantvāna taṃ paṭikaremu accayaṃ, appeva naṃ putta labhemu jīvitaṃ <note>jā. 1.15.13</note>, dajjemu kho <pb ed="M" n="0.0369" /> pañcasatāni bhoto <note>jā. 2.22.1302</note>, pañhaṃ pucchemu mārisa <note>dī. ni. 2.354</note>, viharemu averino <note>dī. ni. 2.357</note>, tayājja guttā viharemu rattinti <note>jā. 1.2.18</note>. Bhaveyyāmu, bhaveyyāma.

Mahāvuttinā kvaci majjhe yyā-kārassa lopo, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi <note>jā. 1.16.150</note>, uregaṇḍāyo bujjhesi, tāyo bujjhesi māṇava <note>jā. 2.17.132-133</note>, yathā gatiṃ me abhisambhavetha <note>jā. 2.17.87-89</note>, yathā gatiṃ te abhisambhavema <note>jā. 2.17.87-89</note>, okāsaṃ sampajānātha, vane yattha vasemaseti <note>jā. 2.22.1885 ‘vasāmase’</note>.

‘Eyyāthasse’iccādisuttena eyyāthassa o ca, tumhe bhaveyyātho, bhaveyyātha vā.

Ettha ca pubbe vuttā pañha, patthanā, vidhippabhedā idhapi yathāpayogaṃ veditabbā. Pañhasaddena paripañha, paripucchā, parivitakka, parivīmaṃsādayo saṅgayhanti.

Paripañhe-dhammaṃ vā paṭhamaṃ saṅgāyeyyāma vinayaṃ vā.

Paripucchāyaṃ-vadetha bhante kimahaṃ kareyyaṃ, ko imassa attho, kathañcassa atthaṃ ahaṃ jāneyyaṃ.

Parivitakke-kassāhaṃ paṭhamaṃ dhammaṃ deseyyaṃ <note>dī. ni. 2.72</note>, yaṃnūnāhaṃ dhammañca vinayañca saṅgāyeyyaṃ <note>pārā. aṭṭha. 1.paṭhamamahāsaṅgītikathā</note>.

Parivīmaṃsāyaṃ-gaccheyyaṃ vā ahaṃ uposathaṃ, na vāgaccheyyaṃ <note>mahāva. 137</note>.

Patthanāyaṃ-evaṃrūpo siyaṃ ahaṃ anāgatamaddhānaṃ <note>ma. ni. 3.274</note>, ummādantyā ramitvāna, sivirājā tato siyaṃ <note>jā. 2.18.70</note>, passeyya taṃ vassasataṃ arogaṃ <note>jā. 2.21.453</note>.

Āyācane-labheyyāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0370" /> bhante bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampadaṃ <note>mahāva. 28; saṃ. ni. 2.17</note>.

Vidhimhi-careyya dhammaṃ <note>jā. 1.14.63</note>.

Niyojane-careyyādittasīsova, natthi maccussa nā gamo <note>saṃ. ni. 1.145</note>.

Ajjhesane-yassa siyā āpatti, so āvikareyya <note>mahāva. 132</note>, yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya <note>mahāva. 70</note>.

Pavāraṇāyaṃ-vadeyyātha bhante yenattho <note>pārā. 290</note>.

Anumatiyaṃ-taṃ jano hareyya vā daheyya vā yathāpaccayaṃ vā kareyya <note>ma. ni. 1.247</note>.

Anuññāyaṃ-ākaṅkhamāno saṅgho kammaṃ kareyya <note>cūḷava. 6</note>.

Āmantane-yadā te pahiṇeyyāmi, tadā eyyāsi khattiya <note>jā. 2.22.635</note>.

Nimantane-idha bhavaṃ nisīdeyya.

Pattakāle-saṅgho uposathaṃ kareyya, pātimokkhaṃ uddiseyya <note>mahāva. 167</note>.

‘Sambhāvane vā’ti vāsaddo avuttavikappanattho, tena parikappa, kriyātipannādayo saṅgayhanti.

Tattha parikappo duvidho bhūtā’bhūtavasena.

Tattha bhūtaparikappe-yo bālaṃ seveyya, sopi bālo bhaveyya.

Abhūtaparikappe-yadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0371" /> kacchapalomānaṃ, pāvāro tividho siyā <note>jā. 1.8.78</note>. Yadā sasavisāṇānaṃ, nisseṇī sukatā siyā <note>jā. 1.8.79</note>.

Kriyātipanne-sace so agāraṃ ajjhāvaseyya, rājā assa cakkavattī <note>dī. ni. 3.136</note>.

Iti eyyādi.

#### Hiyyattanī

Atha hiyyattanī vuccate.

§584. **Anajjattane ā ū o ttha a mhā ttha tthuṃ se vhaṃ iṃ mhase** <note>ka. 418; rū. 456; nī. 886; caṃ. 1.2.77; pā. 3.2.111</note>.

Ajjato aññasmiṃ bhūte kāle kriyatthā paraṃ āiccādayo honti.

§585. **Ā ī ssādīsvaña vā** <note>ka. 519; rū. 457; nī. 1032</note>.

Āiccādīsu īiccādīsu ssādīsu ca tesaṃ ādimhi aña hoti vā.

So abhavā, bhavā, te abhavū, bhavū, tvaṃ abhavo, bhavo, tumhe abhavattha, bhavattha, ahaṃ abhava, bhava, mayaṃ abhavamhā, bhavamhā.

Parachakke-abhavattha, bhavattha, abhavatthuṃ, bhavatthuṃ, abhavase, bhavase, abhavavhaṃ, bhavavhaṃ, abhaviṃ, bhaviṃ, abhavamhase, bhavamhase.

§586. **Ā** <pb ed="M" n="0.0372" /> **ī ū mhā ssā ssāmhānaṃ vā** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Etesaṃ rasso hoti vā.

So abhava, te abhavu, mayaṃ abhavamha.

‘Eyyāthasse’iccādinā āssa tthattaṃ, assa ca aṃ, so abhavattha, bhavattha, abhavā, bhavā vā, ahaṃ abhavaṃ, bhavaṃ, abhava, bhava vā, imāni suddhakatturūpāni.

Ettha ca mahāvuttinā ā-vibhattiyā thādeso bahulaṃ dissati, medanī sampakampatha <note>jā. 2.22.1672</note>, visaññī samapajjatha <note>jā. 2.22.328</note>, imā gāthā abhāsatha <note>jā. 2.22.328</note>, tuccho kāyo adissatha <note>theragā. 172</note>, nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha <note>theragā. 273</note>, eko rahasi jhāyatha <note>jā. 1.15.286</note> iccādi. Tathā o-vibhattiyā ca, dubbheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha iccādi.

Iti hiyyattanī.

#### Ajjattanī

Atha ajjattanī vuccate.

§587. **Bhūte ī uṃ o ttha iṃ mhā ā ū se vhaṃ aṃ mhe** <note>ka. 419; rū. 469; nī. 887</note>.

Abhavīti bhūto, atītoti attho, bhūte kāle kriyatthā paraṃ īiccādayo honti.

§588. **A ī ssā ssatyādīnaṃ byañjanassiu** <note>ka. 516; rū. 466; nī. 1030; caṃ. 1.2.76; pā. 3.2.110 aīssaādīnaṃ byañjanassiu (bahūsu)</note>.

Aādissa īādissa ssāādissa ssatiādissa ca byañjanassa ādimhi iu hoti. ‘Byañjanassā’ti etena aādimhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0373" /> pañca, īādimhi sattāti dvādasa suddhasaravibhattiyo paṭikkhipati.

‘Āīssādīsvaña vā’iti suttena vikappena dhātvādimhi akāro.

So abhavī, bhavī, te abhavuṃ, bhavuṃ, tvaṃ abhavo, bhavo, tumhe abhavittha, bhavittha, ahaṃ abhaviṃ, bhaviṃ, mayaṃ abhavimhā, bhavimhā, so abhavā, bhavā, te abhavū, bhavū, tvaṃ abhavise, bhavise, tumhe abhavivhaṃ, bhavivhaṃ, ahaṃ abhavaṃ, bhavaṃ, mayaṃ abhavimhe, bhavimhe.

‘Āīū’iccādinā ī, mhā, ā, ūnaṃ rassatte-so abhavi, bhavi, mayaṃ abhavimha, bhavimha, so abhava, bhava, te abhavu, bhavu.

§589. **Eyyāthasseaāīthānaṃ o a aṃ ttha ttho vho vā** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105; ‘…vhoka’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Eyyāthādīnaṃ yathākkamaṃ oādayo honti vā.

Tumhe gaccheyyātho, gaccheyyātha vā, tvaṃ agacchissa, agacchisse vā, ahaṃ agamaṃ, gamaṃ, agama, gama vā, so agamittha, gamittha, agamā, gamā vā, so agamittho, gamittho, agamī, gamī vā, tumhe gacchavho, gacchatha vāti.

Iminā ī, ā, avacanānaṃ ttho, ttha, aṃādesā honti, so abhavittho, bhavittho, so abhavittha, bhavittha, ahaṃ abhavaṃ, bhavaṃ.

Atrimā pāḷī – īmhi-paṅko ca mā visiyittho <note>jā. 1.13.44</note>, sañjagghittho mayā saha <note>jā. 1.16.241</note>. Āmhi-anumodittha vāsavo <note>jā. 2.22.1667</note>, nimantayittha <pb ed="M" n="0.0374" /> vāsavo <note>jā. 2.22.1667</note>, khubbhittha nagaraṃ tadā <note>jā. 2.22.1673</note>, subhūtitthero gāthaṃ abhāsittha <note>theragā. 1</note>. Amhi-idhāhaṃ mallikaṃ deviṃ etadavocaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.119</note>, ajānamevaṃ āvuso avacaṃ jānāmīti <note>pārā. 195</note>, ahaṃ kāmānaṃ vasamanvagaṃ <note>jā. 2.19.45</note>, ajjhagaṃ amataṃ santiṃ iccādi.

§590. **Uṃssiṃsvaṃsu** <note>ka. 504, 517; rū. 470-488; nī. 1016-1105</note>.

Umiccassa iṃsu, aṃsu honti.

Agamiṃsu, agamaṃsu, agamuṃ. Iminā uṃssa iṃsu, abhaviṃsu, bhaviṃsu.

§591. **Ossa a i ttha ttho** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Ossa aiccādayo honti.

Tvaṃ abhava, tvaṃ abhavi, tvaṃ abhavittha, tvaṃ abhavittho.

Atrimā pāḷī-ossa atte-mā hevaṃ ānanda avaca <note>dī. ni. 2.95</note>, tvameva dāni’makara, yaṃ kāmo byagamā tayi <note>jā. 1.2.167</note>. Itte-mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja, mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabha <note>jā. 2.22.684</note>, mā cintesi mā tvaṃ soci, yācāmi luddakaṃ ahaṃ <note>gavesitabbaṃ</note>. Tthattemāssu tiṇṇo amaññittha <note>jā. 2.22.255</note>, mā kilittha mayā vinā <note>jā. 2.22.1713</note>, māssu kujjhittha nāvika <note>jā. 1.6.5</note>. Tthotte-mā purāṇe amaññittho <note>theragā. 280</note>, mā dayhittho punappunaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.212</note>, tiṇamatte asajjittho <note>jā. 1.1.89</note>, mā tvaṃ brahmuno vacanaṃ upātivattittho <note>ma. ni. 1.502</note>, mā tvaṃ maññittho na maṃ jānātī <note>ma. ni. 1.502</note> ti.

Tattha <pb ed="M" n="0.0375" /> ‘mā dayhittho’iccādīni parokkhāvacanenapi sijjhanti.

Suttavibhattena tthassa ttho hoti, taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante, yāvantettha samāgatā <note>apa. thera 1.1.367</note>, massu mittānaṃ dubbhittho. Mittadubbho hi pāpakoti <note>jā. 1.16.222</note>.

Mahāvuttinā ossa kvaci lopo, puna dānaṃ adā tuvaṃ <note>jā. 2.22.1786</note>, mā no tvaṃ tāta adadā <note>jā. 2.22.2126</note>, mā bhoti kupitā ahu <note>jā. 2.22.1931</note>, māhu pacchānutāpinī <note>saṃ. ni. 1.162; therīgā. 57</note>.

§592. **Si** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Ossa si hoti vā.

Tvaṃ abhavasi, bhavasi, tvaṃ anubhosi.

§593. **Mhātthānamuu** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Mhā, tthānaṃ ādimhi uña hoti.

Assosumhā, ahesumhā, avocumhā, avocuttha iccādīni dissanti.

Tumhe abhavuttha, bhavuttha, abhavittha, bhavittha vā, mayaṃ abhavumhā, bhavumhā, abhavimhā, bhavimhā vā.

§594. **Iṃssa ca suu** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105; ‘‘…siu’’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Imiccassa mhā, tthānañca ādimhi suu hoti, sāgamo hotīti attho. Casaddena īādīnampi ādimhi sāgamo hoti, sāgame ca sati byañjanaṃ hoti, tassa ādimhi iāgamo labbhati. Tena ‘‘imā gāthā abhāsisuṃ <note>gavesitabbaṃ</note>, te me <pb ed="M" n="0.0376" /> asse ayācisuṃ, yathābhūtaṃ vipassisuṃ’’ <note>jā. 2.22.1863</note> iccādīni <note>dī. ni. 3.277</note> sijjhanti.

So bhogaṃ anubhosi, anubhavi vā, tumhe anubhosittha, anubhavittha vā, ahaṃ anubhosi, anubhaviṃ vā. Mayaṃ anubhosimhā anubhavimhā vā.

§595. **Eontā suṃ** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105; ‘eottā suṃ’’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Edantato odantato ca parassa uṃvacanassa suṃ hoti vā.

Ānesuṃ, sāyesuṃ, cintesuṃ, paccanubhosuṃ, paribhosuṃ, adhibhosuṃ, abhibhosuṃ.

Suttavibhattena ādantatopi ca, vihāsuṃ viharanti ca <note>saṃ. ni. 1.173</note>, te anubhosuṃ, imāni suddhakatturūpāni.

Tena bhogo anvabhūyī, anubhūyī.

Rassatte-anvabhūyi, anubhūyi.

Dvitte-anvabhuyyi, anubhuyyi.

Tena bhogā anvabhūyuṃ, anubhūyuṃ, anvabhūyiṃsu, anubhūyiṃsu iccādi suddhakammarūpaṃ.

So maggaṃ abhāvi, bhāvi, abhāvesi, bhāvesi, abhāvayi, bhāvayi, te maggaṃ abhāviṃsu, bhāviṃsu.

‘Eontāsu’nti edantamhā suṃ. Te maggaṃ abhāvesuṃ, bhāvesuṃ, abhāvayiṃsu, bhāvayiṃsu, tvaṃ maggaṃ abhāvaya, bhāvaya, abhāvayi, bhāvayi, tvaṃ maggaṃ abhāvittha, bhāvittha, abhāvayittha, bhāvayittha, tvaṃ maggaṃ abhāvayittho, bhāvayittho, tvaṃ maggaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0377" /> abhāvesi, bhāvesi, tumhe maggaṃ abhāvittha, bhāvittha, abhāvayittha, bhāvayittha, ahaṃ maggaṃ abhāviṃ, bhāviṃ, abhāvesiṃ, bhāvesiṃ, abhāvayiṃ, bhāvayiṃ, mayaṃ maggaṃ abhāvimhā, bhāvimhā, abhāvimha, bhāvimha, abhāvayimhā, bhāvayimhā, abhāvayimha, bhāvayimha.

So maggaṃ abhāvā, bhāvā, abhāvittha, bhāvittha, abhāvayittha, bhāvayittha iccādi hetukatturūpaṃ.

Tena maggo abhāviyi, bhāviyi, tena maggā abhāviyiṃsu, bhāviyiṃsu iccādi hetukammarūpaṃ.

Iti ajjattanī.

#### Parokkhā

Atha parokkhā vuccate.

§596. **Parokkhe a u e tha aṃ mha ttha re ttho vho iṃ mhe** <note>ka. 417; rū. 460; nī. 887; caṃ. 1.2.81; pā. 3.2.115</note>.

Akkhānaṃ indriyānaṃ paraṃ parokkhaṃ, apaccakkhanti attho. Bhūte kāle attano parokkhakriyāya vattabbāya kriyatthā aādayo honti.

Mahāvuttinā gassa dīgho vā, so kira jagāma, te kira jagāmu, tvaṃ kira jagāme, tumhe kira jagāmittha, ahaṃ kira jagāmaṃ, mayaṃ kira jagāmimha iccādi.

Ettha ca ‘so kira jagāma’ iccādīni **anussavaparokkhāni** nāma.

‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0378" /> kira jagāmaṃ, mayaṃ kira jagāmimhā’ti idaṃ attanā gantvāpi gamanaṃ pamuṭṭhassa vā asampaṭicchitukāmassa vā **paṭivacanaparokkhaṃ** nāma.

§597. **Parokkhāyañca** <note>ka. 458; rū. 461; nī. 939; caṃ. 5.1.3; pā. 6.1.2</note>.

Parokkhamhi pubbakkharaṃ ekassaraṃ dverūpaṃ hoti, casaddena aññasmimpi dvedverūpaṃ sijjhati.

Caṅkamati, daddallati, dadāti, jahāti, juhoti, lolupo, momūho.

§598. **Dutiyacatutthānaṃ paṭhamatatiyā** <note>ka. 461; rū. 464; nī. 942</note>.

Dvitte pubbesaṃ dutiya, catutthānaṃ kamena paṭhama, tatiyā honti.

§599. **Pubbassa a** <note>ka. 450; rū. 463; nī. 946; caṃ. 6.2.126; pā. 7.4.73</note>.

Dvitte pubbassa bhūssa anto a hoti.

§600. **Bhūssa vuka** <note>ka. 475; rū. 465; nī. 956; caṃ. 5.3.92; pā. 6.4.88</note>.

Dvitte bhūdhātussa ante vuka hoti, vāgamo hotīti attho.

‘‘Tatthappanādo tumulo babhūvā’’ti <note>jā. 2.22.1437</note> pāḷi.

So kira rājā babhūva, te kira rājāno babhūvu, tvaṃ babhūve.

‘A ī ssā ssatyādīnaṃ byañjanassiu’ iti suttena byañjanādimhi iāgamo, tumhe babhūvittha, ahaṃ babhūvaṃ, mayaṃ babhūvimha<pb ed="M" n="0.0379" />, so babhūvittha, te babhūvire, tvaṃ babhūvittho, tumhe babhūvivho, ahaṃ babhūviṃ, mayaṃ babhūvimhe, imāni suddhakatturūpāni.

‘Kyo bhāvakammesvaparokkhesū’ti paṭisiddhattā parokkhamhi bhāvakammesu yapaccayo na hoti, ‘tena kira bhogo anubabhūvittha, tena bhogo anubabhūvire’tiādinā yojetabbaṃ.

Iti parokkhā.

#### Ssatyādi

Atha ssatyādi vuccate.

§601. **Bhavissati ssati ssanti ssasi ssatha ssāmi ssāma ssate ssante ssase ssavhe ssaṃ ssāmhe** <note>ka. 421; rū. 473; nī. 892; caṃ. 1.3.2; pā. 3.3.13</note>.

Bhavissatīti bhavissanto, anāgatakālo, tasmiṃ bhavissati kāle kriyatthassa tyādayo honti.

§602. **Nāme garahāvimhayesu** <note>ka. 421; rū. 473; nī. 893; caṃ. 1.3.109, 115; pā. 3.3.143, 150</note>.

Nipātanāmayoge garahāyañca vimhaye ca ssatyādayo honti, atītakālepi ssatyādīnaṃ uppattidīpanatthamidaṃ suttaṃ, anutthunana, paccānutāpa, paccānumodanādīnipi ettha saṅgayhanti.

Tattha garahāyaṃ-atthi nāma tāta sudinna ābhidosikaṃ kummāsaṃ paribhuñjissasi <note>pārā. 32</note>.

Vimhaye-yatra <pb ed="M" n="0.0380" /> hi nāma saññī samāno pañcamattānaṃ sakaṭasatānaṃ saddaṃ na sossati <note>dī. ni. 2.192</note>.

Anutthunanādīsu-na attanā paṭicodessaṃ, na gaṇassa ārocessaṃ <note>pāci. 665</note>, na pubbe dhanamesissaṃ <note>jā. 1.12.50</note>, iti pacchānutappati <note>jā. 1.12.53</note>, bhūtānaṃ nāpacāyissaṃ, pahu santo na posissaṃ, paradāraṃ asevissaṃ <note>jā. 1.12.54</note>, na pubbe payirupāsissaṃ <note>jā. 1.12.58</note>, iti pacchānutappati <note>jā. 1.12.50</note>, anekajātisaṃsāraṃ, sandhāvissaṃ anibbisaṃ <note>dha. pa. 153</note>.

Katthaci pana gāthāvasena ekasakāralopo, mitto mittassa pāniyaṃ, adinnaṃ paribhuñjisaṃ <note>jā. 1.11.59</note>, nirayamhi apaccisaṃ <note>therīgā. 438</note>, gacchanto naṃ udakkhisaṃ <note>gavesitabbaṃ</note>, yoniso paccavekkhisaṃ <note>theragā. 347</note> iccādi.

‘A ī ssā ssatyādīnaṃ byañjanassiu’ iti iāgamo, bhavissati, bhavissanti, bhavissare, bhavissasi, bhavissatha, bhavissāmi, bhavissāma, bhavissate, bhavissante, bhavissare, bhavissase, bhavissavhe, bhavissaṃ, bhavissāmhe.

Anubhossati, anubhossanti, anubhossare iccādi suddhakatturūpaṃ.

Anubhūyissati, anubhūyissanti, anubhūyissare.

§603. **Kyassa sse** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Kyassa lopo hoti vā ssakāravati vibhattimhi.

Tena maggo gamissati, gamīyissati vā, tena maggo agamissā, agamīyissā vāti vikappena kyassa lopo.

Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0381" /> bhogo anubhavissati, anubhūyissati vā, tena bhogā anubhavissanti, anubhūyissanti vā iccādi suddhakammarūpaṃ.

Bhāvissati, ‘ūlasse’ti issa e, bhāvessati, bhāvayissatiiccādi hetukatturūpaṃ.

Tena maggo bhāvīyissati, maggā bhāvīyissanti iccādi hetukammarūpaṃ.

Iti ssatyādi.

#### Ssādi

Atha ssādi vuccate.

§604. **Eyyādotipattiyaṃ ssā ssaṃsu sse ssatha ssaṃ ssāmhā ssatha ssiṃsu ssase ssavhe ssiṃ ssāmhase** <note>ka. 422; rū. 475; nī. 895; caṃ. 1.3.107; pā. 3.3.139; eyyādo vātipattiyaṃ (bahūsu)</note>.

Eyyādivisaye kriyātipattiyaṃ ssādayo bhavanti. Eyyādivisayo nāma hetuphalakriyāsambhavo, tadubhayakriyāya abhāvo kriyātipatti.

Sā duvidhā atītā ca anāgatā ca.

Tattha atītāyaṃ-sace so paṭhamavaye pabbajjaṃ alabhissā, arahā abhavissā <note>‘sace pana nikkhamitvā pabbajissa, arahattaṃ pāpuṇissa’ (dhammapada aṭṭha. 1)</note> iccādi.

Anāgatāyaṃ-sacāhaṃ na gamissaṃ, mahājāniyo so abhavissā iccādi.

‘Āīssādīsvaña <pb ed="M" n="0.0382" /> vā’iti dhātvādimhi vikappena akārāgamo,‘a īssā ssatyādīnaṃ byañjanassiu’ iti ssādīsu iāgamo, abhavissā, bhavissā, abhavissaṃsu, bhavissaṃsu, abhavisse, bhavisse, abhavissatha, bhavissatha, abhavissaṃ, bhavissaṃ, abhavissāmhā, bhavissāmhā, abhavissatha, bhavissatha, abhavissiṃsu, bhavissiṃsu, abhavissase, bhavissase, abhavissavhe, bhavissavhe, abhavissiṃ, bhavissiṃ, abhavissāmhase, bhavissāmhase.

‘Āīū’iccādinā ssā, ssāmhānaṃ rassatte-so abhavissa, bhavissa, mayaṃ abhavissāmha, bhavissāmha. ‘Eyyāthasse’iccādinā ssessa atte-tvaṃ abhavissa, bhavissa iccādīni rūpacatukkāni yathāsambhavaṃ yojetabbāni.

Itissādi.

Bhūdhāturūpaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

Aṭṭhavibhattuppattirāsi niṭṭhito.

#### Bhūvādigaṇa

#### Sarantadhātu

#### Ākārantadhāturūpa

Ito paṭṭhāya sarantadhātuyo sarānukkamena, byañjanantadhātuyo akkharānukkamena vuccante.

Kaccāyanaganthe anekassaradhātuyo idha byañjanantadhātuyo nāma. Tasmā idha dhātvantasaralopakiccaṃ nāma natthi.

Khā, khyā-kathane, gā-sadde, ghā-gandhopādāne, ñā-paññāyane avabodhane ca, ṭhā-gatinivattiyaṃ, tā-pālane, thā-ṭhāne<pb ed="M" n="0.0383" />, dā-dāne, dhā-dhāraṇe, pā-pāne, phā-vuddhiyaṃ, bhā-dittiyaṃ, mā-māne, yā-gatiyaṃ, lā-ādāne chedane ca, vā-gati, bandha, gandhanesu, sā-assādane tanukaraṇe antakammani ca, hā-cāge, nhā-soceyye.

Tyādyuppatti, kattarilo, mahāvuttinā sare pare ādantamhā kvaci yāgamo, akkhāti. Parassaralopo, akkhāyati, kriyaṃ ākhyāti, ākhyāyati, jātiṃ akkhāhi pucchito <note>su. ni. 423</note>, saṅgāyati, saṅgāyiṃsu mahesayo <note>vi. va. aṭṭha. ganthārambhakathā</note>, gandhaṃ ghāyati, paññāyati, paññāyanti, paññāyatu, paññāyantu.

Kamme kyo, dhammo ñāyati, dhammā ñāyanti, viññāyati, viññāyanti.

Payojakabyāpāre-ṇāpi, ñāpeti, ñāpenti, ñāpayati, ñāpayanti.

Kamme-ñāpīyati, ñāpīyanti, ṭhāti, ṭhānti, opupphā padmā ṭhānti, mālāva ganthitā ṭhānti, dhajaggāneva dissare <note>jā. 2.22.1989</note>.

§605. **Ñcīlasse** <note>ka. 510; rū. 487; nī. 1023</note>.

Ñānubandhassa īāgamassa ca kattari vihitassa lapaccayassa ca kvaci ettaṃ hotīti lassa ettaṃ.

Adhiṭṭheti, adhiṭṭhenti.

§606. **Ṭhāpānaṃ tiṭṭhapivā** <note>ka. 468-9; rū. 492-4; nī. 949</note>.

Ṭhā, pānaṃ tiṭṭha, pivā honti nta, māna, tyādīsu.

Tiṭṭhati, tiṭṭhanti.

§607. **Pādito ṭhāssa vā ṭhaho kvaci** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Pādayo <pb ed="M" n="0.0384" /> upasaggā pādi nāma, pādito parassa ṭhāssa ṭhaho hoti vā kvaci.

Saṇṭhahati, saṇṭhahanti, saṇṭhāti, saṇṭhānti, upaṭṭhahati, upaṭṭhahanti, upaṭṭhāti, upaṭṭhānti.

Kamme –

§608. **Aññādissi kye** <note>ka. 502; rū. 493; nī. 1015; ‘aññādissāsīkye’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Ñādito aññassa ākārantakriyatthassa i hoti kye paramhi.

Adhiṭṭhīyati, adhiṭṭhīyanti, upaṭṭhīyati, upaṭṭhīyanti.

Aññādissāti kiṃ? Ñāyati, ñāyanti, ākkhāyati, ākkhāyanti, ākhyāyati, ākhyāyanti.

Ṇāpimhi-patiṭṭhāpeti, patiṭṭhāpenti, patiṭṭhāpayati, patiṭṭhāpayanti.

Ajjhattanimhi vikappena sāgamo, aṭṭhāsi, patiṭṭhāsi, adhiṭṭhahi, adhiṭṭhāsi, adhiṭṭhesi, saṇṭhahi, saṇṭhāsi, upaṭṭhahi, upaṭṭhāsi.

‘Uṃssiṃsvaṃsū’ti uṃssa iṃsu, aṃsu, adhiṭṭhahiṃsu, saṇṭhahiṃsu, upaṭṭhahiṃsu. Atthamentamhi sūriye, vāḷā panthe upaṭṭhahuṃ <note>jā. 2.22.2186</note>. Aṭṭhaṃsu, upaṭṭhahaṃsu.

Parachakke-aṭṭhā buddhassa santike <note>su. ni. 431</note>.

Kamme-adhiṭṭhiyi, adhiṭṭhiyiṃsu, upaṭṭhiyi, upaṭṭhiyiṃsu.

Ṇāpimhi-patiṭṭhāpesi<pb ed="M" n="0.0385" />, patiṭṭhāpayi, saṇṭhāpesi, saṇṭhāpayi.

‘Eontāsu’nti uṃssasuṃ, saralopo, aṭṭhāsuṃ, upaṭṭhāsuṃ, patiṭṭhāpesuṃ, saṇṭhāpesuṃ, patiṭṭhāpayuṃ, saṇṭhāpayuṃ, patiṭṭhāpayiṃsu, saṇṭhāpayiṃsu.

Ssatyādimhi-ṭhassati, ṭhassanti, rassattaṃ, upaṭṭhissati, upaṭṭhissanti, ahaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ <note>jā. 2.22.1934</note>, saṇṭhahissati, saṇṭhahissanti.

Ṇāpimhi-patiṭṭhāpessati, patiṭṭhāpessanti.

Tā-pālane, bhayaṃ tāyati.

Thā-ṭhāne, avatthāti, avatthāyati, vitthāyati, vitthāyanti, mā kho vitthāsi <note>mahāva. 126</note>.

Dā-dāne, ‘ūlasse’ti lassa ettaṃ, deti, denti, desi, detha, demi, dema.

‘Parokkhāyañcā’ti sutte casaddena dāssa dvittaṃ. ‘Rasso pubbassā’ti pubbassa rassattaṃ, dadāti, dadanti, dadāsi, dadātha, dadāmi, dadāma.

§609. **Dāssa daṃ vā mimesvadvitte** <note>ka. 482; rū. 508; nī. 972</note>.

Advitte dāssa daṃ hoti vā mi, mesu, niggahītassa vaggantattaṃ.

Dammi, damma.

Advitteti kiṃ? Dadāmi, dadāma.

§610. **Dāssiyaṅa** <note>ka. 502; rū. 493; nī. 1014</note>.

Pādito <pb ed="M" n="0.0386" /> parassa dāssa iyaṅa hoti kvaci.

‘Iyaṅa’ iti suttavibhattena aññadhātūnampi. Jā-hāniyaṃ, appena bahuṃ jiyyāma <note>jā. 1.2.52</note>, tassevā’nuvidhiyyati <note>jā. 1.2.67</note>, vidhurassa hadayaṃ dhaniyati <note>jā. 2.22.1350</note>, nihīyati tassa yaso <note>jā. 1.10.60; a. ni. 4.17</note>, eko rājā vihiyyasi <note>jā. 2.22.1750</note>, so pahīyissati <note>saṃ. ni. 1.249</note> iccādi.

Ādiyati, ādiyanti, upādiyati, upādiyanti, samādiyati, samādiyanti, sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi <note>khu. pā. 2.1</note>, vattaṃ samādiyāmi <note>cūḷava. 85</note>.

§611. **Gama vada dānaṃ ghamma vajja dajjā** <note>ka. 499-500-1; rū. 443-486-507; nī. 1013, 1005-1006</note>.

Etesaṃ ghamma, vajja, dajjā honti vā nta, māna, tyādīsu.

‘Ūlasse’ti lassa ettaṃ, dajjeti, dajjenti.

Kamme ‘aññādissi kye’ti kyamhi āssa ittaṃ, diyati, diyanti.

Dīghatte-dīyati, dīyanti.

Dvitte-diyyati, diyyanti, dajjīyati, dajjīyanti.

Ṇāpimhi-dāpeti, dāpenti, dāpayati, dāpayanti.

Pādipubbe rasso, samādapeti <note>ma. ni. 2.387; 3.276</note>, samādapenti, samādapayati, samādapayanti.

Kamme-dāpīyati<pb ed="M" n="0.0387" />, dāpīyanti, samādapīyati, samādapīyanti.

Eyyādimhi mahāvuttinā dajjato eyyādīnaṃ antassa eyyassa lopo vā, dānaṃ dajjā, dadeyya, dajjuṃ, dadeyyuṃ, dajjāsi, dadeyyāsi, dajjātha, dadeyyātha, dajjāmi, dadeyyāmi, dajjāma, dadeyyāma, ahaṃ dajjaṃ, dadeyyaṃ, mayaṃ dajjāmhe, dadeyyāmhe.

Atrimā pāḷī-dajjā sappuriso dānaṃ <note>jā. 2.22.2261</note>, upāyanāni me dajjuṃ <note>jā. 2.22.24</note>, mātaraṃ kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino <note>jā 1.16.227</note>. Tāni ammāya dajjesi <note>jā. 2.22.2149</note>, chaṭṭhāhaṃ dajjamattānaṃ, neva dajjaṃ mahosadhaṃ <note>jā. 1.16.225</note>.

Ajjhattanimhi-adadi, adāsi, adaduṃ, adaṃsu, adajji, adajjuṃ, tvaṃ adado. Varañce me ado sakka <note>jā. 2.17.142</note>.

Parachakke-so dānaṃ adā, brāhmaṇassa adā dānaṃ, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano <note>jā. 2.22.2117</note>.

Ssatyādimhi-dāssati, dāssanti, dadissati, dadissanti, dajjissati, dajjissanti.

Dāiccassa diccha, pavecchādesampi icchanti, vipulaṃ annaṃ pānañca, samaṇānaṃ pavecchasi <note>therīgā. 272</note>. Appasmeke pavecchanti, bahuneke na dicchare <note>saṃ. ni. 1.33</note>. Devo sammā dhāraṃ pavecchatu. Bhojanaṃ bhojanatthīnaṃ, sammadeva pavecchatha.

Dhā-dhāraṇe, sandhāti, vidhāti, nidheti, nidhenti. Vidheti, vidhenti.

‘Parokkhāyañcā’ti casaddena dvittaṃ. ‘Dutiyacatutthāna…’nti dhassa dattaṃ. ‘Rasso pubbassā’ti pubbassa rasso.

§612. **Dhāssa ho** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Dvitte <pb ed="M" n="0.0388" /> parassa dhāssa ho hoti.

Saddahāti, saddahati vā. Saddahāti tathāgatassa bodhiṃ. Vidahāti, nidahāti, saddahanti, vidahanti, nidahanti.

‘Mayadā sare’ti sutte ‘mayadā’ti suttavibhattiyā byañjanepi niggahītassa dattaṃ, kammaṃ saddahāti, kammaphalaṃ saddahāti, saddahanti, vatthaṃ paridahāti, paridahanti.

Kamme-sandhīyati, sandhīyanti, sandhiyyati, sandhiyyanti, vidhiyyati. Navena sukhadukkhena, porāṇaṃ apidhiyyati <note>jā. 1.2.114</note>.

Ṇāpimhi-nidhāpeti, nidhāpenti, nidhāpayati, nidhāpayanti.

Kamme-nidhāpīyati, nidhāpīyanti.

Eyyādimhi-saddaheyyaṃ, saddaheyyuṃ.

Īādimhi-saddahi, saddahiṃsu. Tatra bhikkhavo samādahiṃsu <note>dī. ni. 2.332</note>, samādahaṃsu vā.

Pā-pāne, pāti, pānti.

‘Ṭhāpānaṃ tiṭṭhapivā’ti pāssa pivo, pivati, pivanti.

Kamme-pīyati, pīyanti.

Ṇimhi-‘āssā ṇāpimhi yuka’ iti suttena ṇānubandhe āssa ante yāgamo, puttaṃ thaññaṃ pāyeti, pāyenti, pāyayati, pāyayanti.

Kamme-pāyīyati, pāyīyanti.

Ssatyādimhi-passati, passanti, pissati, pissanti.

Atrimā <pb ed="M" n="0.0389" /> pāḷī-ayañhi te mayā’ruḷho, saro pissati lohitaṃ <note>jā. 2.22.1968</note>,aggodakāni pissāmi, yūthassa purato vajaṃ <note>jā. 1.8.14</note>. Naḷena vāriṃ pissāma, na ca maṃ tvaṃ vadhissasi <note>jā. 1.1.20</note>.

Bhā-dittiyaṃ, bhāti, rattimābhāti candimā <note>dha. pa. 387</note>, disā bhanti virocamānā <note>ma. ni. 1.503</note>, daddallamānā ābhanti <note>vi. va. 738; jā. 2.22.508</note>, paṭibhāti, paṭibhanti, paṭibhātu, paṭibhantu taṃ cunda bojjhaṅgā <note>saṃ. ni. 5.197</note>, tisso maṃ upamāyo paṭibhaṃsu <note>ma. ni. 1.374</note>, ratti vibhāti, vibhāyati.

Mā-māne, dvittaṃ rasso ca, mamāyati, mamāyanti. Yemaṃ kāyaṃ mamāyanti, andhā bālā puthujjanā <note>theragā. 575</note>.

Yā-gatiyaṃ, yāti, yanti, yāyati, yāyanti, yāyanta’ manuyāyanti <note>jā. 2.22.1753</note>, uyyāti, uyyanti, niyyāti, niyyanti dhīrā lokamhā, hitvā māraṃ savāhanaṃ. Anuyāti, anuyanti, anupariyāyati, anupariyāyanti.

Lā-ādāne, lāti.

Vā-gati, gandhanesu, vāti devesu uttamo <note>dha. pa. 56</note>, vāto vāyati, vāyanti, nibbāti, nibbanti, nibbāyati, nibbāyanti, parinibbāti, parinibbāyati.

Ṇāpimhi-nibbāpeti, nibbāpayati.

Īādimhi-parinibbāyi, parinibbāyiṃsu.

Ssatyādimhi-parinibbissati, parinibbissanti, parinibbāyissati, parinibbāyissanti.

Sā-assādana, tanukaraṇa, antakriyāsu, sāti, sāyati, sāyanti, pariyosāyanti.

Ṇāpimhi-osāpeti<pb ed="M" n="0.0390" />, pariyosāpeti, osāpayati, pariyosāpayati.

Kamme-osāpīyati, pariyosāpīyati.

Hā-cāge, pahāti, pahāyati, pahāyanti.

Kattu, kammani kyo, īñaāgamo, hiyyoti hiyyati poso <note>jā. 1.15.348</note>, nihiyyati tassa yaso <note>a. ni. 4.17; jā. 1.10.60</note>, tvaṃ eko avahiyyasi, dvittaṃ rasso ca.

§613. **Kavaggahānaṃ cavaggajā** <note>ka. 462-4; rū. 467-504; nī. 943-5; caṃ. 6.2.116; pā. 7.4.62</note>.

Dvitte pubbesaṃ kavagga, hānaṃ cavagga, jā honti.

Jahāti, pajahāti, jahanti, pajahanti.

Kamme-pahīyati, pahīyanti.

Ṇāpimhi-hāpeti, hāpenti, hāpayati, hāpayanti, jahāpeti, jahāpenti, jahāpayati, jahāpayanti.

Kamme-hāpīyati, jahāpīyati.

Īādimhi-pahāsi, pahāsuṃ, pajahi, pajahiṃsu.

§614. **Hāto ha** <note>ka. 480; rū. 490; nī. 961</note>.

Hāto parassa ssa-kārassa ha hoti vā.

‘‘Hāhisi <pb ed="M" n="0.0391" /> tvaṃ jīvaloka’’nti <note>jā. 1.5.36</note> pāḷi, hāhiti, hāhinti, hāhati, hāhanti, jahissati, hissati, aññamaññaṃ vadhitvāna, khippaṃ hissāma jīvitaṃ <note>jā. 2.22.673</note>.

Nhā-soceyye, nhāti, nhāyati, nhāyanti.

Mahāvuttinā byañjanavaḍḍhane, nahāti, nahāyati, nahāyanti.

Iti bhūvādigaṇe ākārantadhāturūpaṃ.

#### Ivaṇṇantadhāturūpa

I-gatiyaṃ ajjhāyane ca, khi-khaye pakāsane ca, cicaye, ji-jaye, ḍī-vehāsagatiyaṃ, nī-naye, bhī-bhaye, lī-laye, sī-saye, mhi-hāse.

Tyādyuppatti, kattari lo, eti, enti, esi, etha, emi, ema, veti, venti, sameti, samenti, abbheti, abbhenti, abhisameti, abhisamenti, aveti, aventi, samaveti, samaventi, apeti, apenti, upeti, upenti, anveti, anventi, acceti, accenti, pacceti, paccenti, ajjheti, ajjhenti, udeti, udenti, samudeti, samudenti, pariyeti, pariyenti, upayati, upayanti, accayati, accayanti, udayati, samudayati.

Etu, sametu, entu, samentu, ehi, samehi, etha, sametha, etha byagghā nivattavho, paccupetha mahāvanaṃ <note>jā. 1.3.66</note>.

Mahāvuttinā idhātumhā eyyādīnaṃ ekārassa lopo, na ca apatvā dukkhassantaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.107</note>, vissāsaṃ eyya paṇḍito, yadā te pahiṇeyyāmi, tadā eyyāsi khattiya <note>jā. 2.22.635</note>.

Īādimhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0392" /> ‘paro kvacī’ti vibhattisaralopo, dhammaṃ abhisami, abhisamiṃsu.

‘Eontā su’nti uṃssa suṃ, abhisamesuṃ, abhisamayuṃ, abhisamayiṃsu.

Ssatyādimhi –

§615. **Etismā** <note>ka. 480; rū. 490; nī. 961</note>.

‘Etī’ti dhātuniddeso tisaddo, idhātumhā parassa ssakārassa hi hoti vā.

Ehiti, essati. Bodhirukkhamupehiti <note>bu. vaṃ. 2.63</note>, nerañjaramupehiti <note>bu. vaṃ. 2.63</note>, upessati, tadā ehinti me vasaṃ <note>jā. 1.1.33</note>, tato nibbānamehisi <note>cūḷava. 382 tassuddānaṃ</note>, na punaṃ jātijaraṃ upehisi <note>dha. pa. 238</note>. Suttavibhattena aññadhātūhipi, kathaṃ jīvihisi tvaṃ <note>apa. thera 1.3.13</note>, jāyihitippasādo <note>jā. 2.17.145</note>, paññāyihinti etā daharā <note>jā. 2.17.197</note>.

Ssādimhi ‘‘sace puttaṃ siṅgālānaṃ, kukkurānaṃ adāhisī’’ti <note>gavesitabbaṃ</note> pāḷi, ‘adāhisī’ti ca adadissasetyattho.

Khi-khaye avaṇṇapakāsane ca, khayati, khayanti.

Khito yāgamo, vikappena yassa dvittaṃ, kappo khīyetha, vaṇṇo na khīyetha tathāgatassa <note>dī. ni. aṭṭha. 1.304</note>, ujjhāyanti khīyanti <note>pārā. 88</note>, avaṇṇaṃ pakāsentīti attho. Khiyyati, khiyyanti, āyu khiyyati maccānaṃ, kunnadīnaṃva odakaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.146</note>.

Ci-caye, samucceti, samuccayati.

§616. **Nito cissa cho** <note>ka. 20; rū. 27; nī. 50</note>.

Nito <pb ed="M" n="0.0393" /> parassa cissa ca-kārassa cho hoti.

Nicchayati, vinicchayati, vinicchayanti, viniccheti, vinicchenti,

Kamme kyo –

§617. **Dīgho sarassa** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Sarantassa dhātussa dīgho hoti kyamhīti ikāru’kārānaṃ kyamhi vikappena dīgho.

Samuccīyati samuccīyanti, vinicchīyati, vinicchīyanti.

Ji-jaye, jeti, jenti, vijeti, vijenti, parājeti, parājenti, jayati, jayanti, vijayati, vijayanti, parājayati, parājayanti.

Kamme kyamhi dīgho, na taṃ jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ avajīyati. Taṃ kho jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ nāvajīyati <note>jā. 1.1.70</note>.

Ṇāpimhi pubbassaralopo vā, jāpeti, jāpayati. Yo na hanti na ghāteti, na jināti na jāpaye <note>jā. 1.10.144</note>. Jayāpeti, jayāpayati, jayāpīyati, jayāpīyanti, jayatu, jayantu.

Īādimhi-ajesi, ajesuṃ, vijesi, vijesuṃ, ajayi, ajayuṃ, ajayiṃsu, vijayi, vijayuṃ, vijayiṃsu, jessati, vijessati, parājessati, jayissati, vijayissati, parājayissati.

Ḍī-vehāsagatiyaṃ, sakuṇo ḍeti, ḍenti <note>dī. ni. 1.215; a. ni. 4.198</note>. Pāsaṃ oḍḍeti, oḍḍenti.

Nī-naye<pb ed="M" n="0.0394" />, neti, nenti, vineti, vinenti, nayati, nayanti, vinayati, vinayanti.

Kamme-nīyati, nīyanti.

Dvitte-niyyati, niyyanti, niyyare.

Ṇāpimhi āyādesassa rasso, nayāpeti, nayāpenti, nayāpayati, nayāpayanti.

Kamme-nayāpīyati, nayāpīyanti.

Īādimhi-nesi, nesuṃ, vinesi, vinesuṃ, ānesi, ānesuṃ, anayi, nayi, anayiṃsu, nayiṃsu, ānayi, ānayiṃsu, vinayi, vinayiṃsu.

Ssatyādimhi-nessati, nessanti, nayissati, nayissanti.

Bhī-bhaye, bheti. Mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathavho <note>jā. 1.12.27</note>, vibhemi etaṃ asādhuṃ, uggatejo hi brāhmaṇo <note>jā. 2.17.103</note>. Bhāyati, bhāyanti.

Kārite mahāvuttinā sāgamo vā, bhīseti, bhīsayati, bhīsāpeti, bhīsāpayati. Bhikkhuṃ bhīseyya vā bhīsāpeyya vā <note>pāci. 346-347</note>.

Sī-saye, seti, senti, atiseti, atisenti, sayati, sayanti.

Kamme-atisīyati, atisīyanti.

Ṇāpimhi rasso, sayāpeti, sayāpayati.

Ṇimhi-sāyeti, sāyayati, sāyesuṃ dīnamānasā <note>apa. thera 2.54.48</note>.

Mhi-hāse<pb ed="M" n="0.0395" />, umheti, umhayati, vimheti, vimhayati, na naṃ umhayate disvā, na ca naṃ paṭinandati <note>jā. 1.2.93</note>.

Kamme-umhīyati, vimhīyati.

Kārite pubbassaralopo, sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, umhāyeyya pabhāvatī. Sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, pamhāyeyya pabhāvatī <note>jā. 2.20.17</note>.

Iti bhūvādigaṇe ivaṇṇantadhārūpaṃ.

#### Uvaṇṇantadhāturūpa

Cu-cavane, ju-sīghagamane, thu-abhitthavane, du-gatiyaṃ upatāpe ca, bhū-sattāyaṃ, yu-missane gatiyañca, ru-sadde, brū-viyattiyaṃ vācāyaṃ, su-sandane janane ca, sū-pasavane, hu-dāne bhakkhane pūjāyaṃ sattiyañca, hū-sattāyaṃ.

Tyādyuppatti, ‘kattari lo’ti lapaccayo, uvaṇṇassa avādeso, ‘dīgho sarassā’ti sakammikadhātūnaṃ kyamhi dīgho.

Cu-cavane, cavati, cavanti.

Ṇimhi-cāveti, cāvayati.

Ju-sīghagamane, javati, javanti.

Thu-abhitthavane, abhitthavati, abhitthavanti.

‘Bahula’nti adhikatattā kyamhi kvaci vuddhi, avādeso, abhitthavīyati, abhitthavīyanti, abhitthaviyyati, abhitthaviyyanti.

Du-upatāpe, upaddavati, upaddavanti.

Bhū-sattāyaṃ, sambhoti, sambhavati.

Yu-gatiyaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0396" />, yavati.

Ru-sadde, ravati, ravanti, viravati, viravanti.

Brū-viyattiyaṃ vācāyaṃ –

§618. **Na brūsso**.

Byañjane pare brūssa o na hoti.

Brūti.

§619. **Brūto tissīu** <note>ka. 520; rū. 502; nī. 1033; caṃ. 6.2.34; pā. 7.3.93</note>.

Brūto tissa ādimhi īña hoti. Īmhi pubbalopo.

Bravīti.

§620. **Yuvaṇṇānamiyaṅauvaṅa sare** <note>ka. 70; rū. 30; nī. 220; …miyavuvaṅa… (bahūsu)</note>.

Ivaṇṇu’vaṇṇantānaṃ dhātūnaṃ kvaci iyaṅa, uvaṅa honti sare.

Bruvanti, brunti vā. ‘‘Ajānantā no pabruntī’’ti pāḷi. Brūsi, brūtha, brūmi, brūma.

§621. **Tyantīnaṃ ṭaṭū** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105; caṃ. 1.4.13; pā. 3.4.84</note>.

Ti, antīsu brūssa āha hoti, tesañca ṭa, ṭū honti.

So āha, te āhu.

Atrimā pāḷī-nibbānaṃ bhagavā āha, sabbaganthapamocanaṃ, āha tesañca yo nirodho <note>mahāva. 60</note>, yaṃ pare sukhato āhu, tadariyā āhu dukkhato. Yaṃ pare dukkhato āhu, tadariyā sukhato vidū <note>su. ni. 767</note>. Tattha ‘āhā’ti katheti. ‘Āhū’ti kathenti.

Brūtu<pb ed="M" n="0.0397" />, brūvantu, brūhi maṅgalamuttamaṃ <note>khu. pā. 5.2</note>, brūtha, brūmi, brūma.

Eyyādimhi-brūssa uvaṅa hoti, bruveyya, bruveyyuṃ.

Īādimhi sare pare brūssa ottaṃ, ossa ca avādeso, abravi, abravuṃ, abraviṃsu.

Uvādese-abruvi, abruvuṃ, abruviṃsu.

Parokkhamhi –

§622. **Aādīsvāho brūssa** <note>ka. 475; rū. 465; nī. 956</note>.

Aādīsu brūssa āha bhavati.

So āha, te āhu.

§623. **Ussaṃsvāhā vā** <note>nī. 1036</note>.

Āhādesamhā parassa uvacanassa aṃsu hoti vā.

Te āhaṃsu, saccaṃ kirevamāhaṃsu, narā ekacciyā idha <note>jā. 1.13.123</note>.

Su-sandane, nadī savati, savanti, ābhavaggā savanti.

Sū-pasavane, puññaṃ pasavati <note>cūḷava. 354</note>, pasavanti.

Hu-pūjāyaṃ, ‘parokkhāyañcā’ti dvittaṃ, ‘kavaggahānaṃ cavaggajā’ti hassa jo, juhoti, juhonti.

Kamme-tena aggi hūyate.

Ṇimhi-juhāveti, juhāvayati.

Ṇāpimhi-juhāpeti, juhāpayati.

Hu-sattiyaṃ, pahoti, sampahoti, pahonti, sampahonti.

Hū-sattāyaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0398" />, hoti, honti, hotu, hontu.

Eyyādimhi- ‘yuvaṇṇānamiyaṅauvaṅa sare’ti dhātvantassa uvādeso, huveyya, huveyyuṃ.

Āādimhi-so ahuvā. Vaṇṇagandhaphalūpeto, amboyaṃ ahuvā pure <note>jā. 1.2.71</note>. Ahuvā te pure sakhā <note>saṃ. ni. 1.50</note>, te ahuvū, tvaṃ ahuvo, tumhe ahuvattha <note>ma. ni. 1.215</note>, jhāyatha bhikkhave mā pamādāttha, mā pacchā vippaṭisārino ahuvattha, ahuva, ahuvaṃ vā, ahuvamhā. ‘‘Akaramhasa te kiccaṃ, yaṃ balaṃ ahuvamhase <note>jā. 1.4.29</note>. Ahuvamheva mayaṃ pubbe, na nāhuvamhā’’ti <note>ma. ni. 1.180</note> pāḷiyo.

Īādimhi sāgamo, ahosi, pāturahosi.

Mahāvuttinā īlopo rasso ca. Ahudeva bhayaṃ ahu chambhitattaṃ. Ahudeva kukkuccaṃ, ahu vippaṭisāro <note>pārā. 38</note>. Ādīnavo pāturahu <note>theragā. 269</note>, dibbo ratho pāturahu.

§624. **Hūto resuṃ** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Hūto ñuṃvacanassa resuṃ hoti. Suttavibhattena mhāssa resumhā ca. ‘Rānubandhentasarādissā’ti dhātvantalopo.

Te pubbe ahesuṃ. Uvādese ahuvuṃ, pubbassaralope ahuṃ.

Atrimā pāḷī- sabbamhi taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha dijā ahuṃ <note>jā. 2.22.2425</note>. Kūṭāgārasahassāni, sabbasoṇṇamayā ahuṃ <note>apa. thera 1.1.407</note>.

Ossa <pb ed="M" n="0.0399" /> si, ittha, ttho. Tvaṃ ahosi, ahuvi, ahuvittha, ahuvittho.

Mahāvuttinā olopo rasso, mā bhoti kupitā ahu <note>jā. 2.22.1931</note>, māhu pacchānutāpinī <note>saṃ. ni. 1.162</note>, ahosiṃ nu kho ahaṃ atītamaddhānaṃ, na nu kho ahosiṃ, kinnu kho ahosiṃ, kathaṃ nu kho ahosiṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 2.20; ma. ni. 1.18</note>, ahaṃ ahuviṃ, mayaṃ ahosimhā, ahosimha vā. Ahesumhā nu kho mayaṃ atītamaddhānaṃ, na nu kho ahesumhā, kinnu kho ahesumhā, kathaṃ nu kho ahesumhā <note>ma. ni. 1.407</note>. Mayaṃ pubbe ahuvimhā, ahumhā vā. ‘‘Mayaṃ pubbe dānapatino ahumhā’’ti <note>jā. 2.22.1617</note> pāḷi.

Rassatte-ahumha.

Mahāvuttinā mhāssa uñca. ‘‘Pañcasatā mayaṃ sabbā, tāvatiṃsupagā ahu’’nti pāḷi.

Parachakke assa aṃ, ahaṃ pubbe ahuvaṃ, ahuva vā.

‘Paro kvacī’ti paralopo, ahuṃ.

Atrimā pāḷī- ‘‘ahaṃ kevaṭṭagāmasmiṃ, ahuṃ kevaṭṭadārako <note>apa. thera 1.39.86</note>, cakkavattī ahuṃ rājā, jambumaṇḍassa issaro. Sattakkhattuṃ mahābrahmā, vasavattī tadā ahuṃ. Muddhābhisitto khattiyo, manussādhipatī ahu’’nti. Mayaṃ ahuvimhe.

Ssatyādimhi –

§625. **Hūssa hehehihohi ssaccādo** <note>ka. 480; rū. 490; nī. 961; ‘…ssatyādo’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Ssatyādimhi hūdhātussa he ca hohi ca hohi ca honti.

Hessati<pb ed="M" n="0.0400" />, hessanti, hehissati, hehissanti, hohissati, hohissanti. Buddho hessaṃ sadevake <note>bu. vaṃ. 2.55</note>, anāgatamhi addhāne, hessāma sammukhā imaṃ <note>bu. vaṃ. 2.74</note>.

§626. **Dakkha sakkha hehi hohīhi lopo** <note>ka. 480; rū. 490; nī. 961; ‘dakkhā hehihohilopo’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Etehi ādesehi ssassa lopo hoti vā. Suttavibhattena aññehipi ssalopo.

Sakkhisi tvaṃ kuṇḍalini, maññisi khattabandhuni <note>jā. 2.17.14</note>. Na hi sakkhinti chettuṃ <note>su. ni. 28</note>, adhammo haññiti dhammamajja <note>jā. 1.11.31</note>, brahmadatto palāyiti iccādi.

Hehiti, hehinti, hohiti, hohinti.

Atrimā pāḷī-piyo ca me hehiti mālabhārī, ahañca naṃ mālinī ajjhupessaṃ <note>jā. 1.15.197</note>, tilodano hehiti sādhupakko <note>jā. 1.8.2</note>. Doso pemañca hehiti <note>theragā. 719</note>. Mama tvaṃ hehisi bhariyā <note>jā. 1.14.27</note>. Tato sukhī hohisi vītarāgo. Khippaṃ hohisi anāsavo <note>dī. ni. 2.207</note> iccādi.

Iti bhūvādigaṇe uvaṇṇantadhāturūpaṃ.

#### Edantadhāturūpa

E-āgatiyaṃ gatiyañca, ke-sadde, khe-khādanu’paṭṭhānesu, ge-sadde, apapubba ce-pūjāyaṃ, jhe-cintāyaṃ dāha’jjhānesu ca, te-pālane, the-sadda, saṅghātesu, de-suddhi, niddāsu, pe-vuddhiyaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0401" />, bhe-bhaye, le-chedane, ve-gatiyaṃ tantasantāne ca, se-antakriyāyaṃ, hare-lajjāyaṃ, gile-kilamane, pale-gatiyaṃ, mile-hāniyaṃ.

Ṇānubandhapaccayena vinā yesaṃ dhātūnaṃ āyādeso labbhati, te edantā nāma. Mahāvuttinā yalope sati ādantehi samānarūpaṃ, ādantānañca yāgame sati edantehi samānarūpaṃ, tasmā ādanta, edantā yebhuyyena samānarūpā bhavanti.

Mahāvuttinā edantānaṃ tyādīsu tabbādīsu ca āyādeso, kvaci yalopo, e-āgatiyaṃ. Ayaṃ so sārathī eti <note>jā. 2.22.51</note>, sace enti manussattaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.49</note>, lakkhaṇaṃ passa āyantaṃ, migasaṅghapurakkhataṃ <note>jā. 1.1.11</note>, yoga’māyanti maccuno <note>saṃ. ni. 1.20</note>, āyāmāvuso <note>pārā. 228</note>, āyāmānanda <note>dī. ni. 2.186; pārā. 22; ma. ni. 1.273</note>.

Ettha edhātu āgaccha, gacchāmāti atthadvayaṃ vadati, yādhātuvasena āgaccha, yāmātipi atthaṃ vadanti.

E-vuddhiyaṃ vā, ‘‘kāyo, apāyo, upāyo, samudāyo’’tiādīsu –

Kucchitā dhammā āyanti vaḍḍhanti etthāti kāyo, ‘āyo’ti vuccati vaḍḍhi, tato apeto apāyo, tena upeto upāyo, avayavadhammā samudenti etthāti samudāyo, paribyattaṃ āyanti etenāti pariyāyo.

Ke-sadde, kāyati.

Kamme-kiyyati.

Khe-khādane, tiṇaṃ khāyati, vikkhāyati, undurā khāyanti, vikkhāyanti.

Khe-upaṭṭhāne<pb ed="M" n="0.0402" />, khāyati, pakkhāyati, alakkhī viya khāyati.

Ge-sadde, gāyati, gāyanti.

Apapubba ce-pūjāyaṃ, apacāyati, ye vuddha’mapacāyanti <note>jā. 1.1.37</note>.

Jhe-cintāyaṃ, jhāyati, jhāyanti, pajjhāyati, pajjhāyanti, abhijjhāyati, abhijjhāyanti.

Jhe-olokane, nijjhāyati, nijjhāyanti, upanijjhāyati, upanijjhāyanti, ujjhāyati, ujjhāyanti.

Jhe-dayhane, padīpo jhāyati, parijjhāyati.

Kamme-jhāyīyati.

Ṇāpimhi yalopo, kaṭṭhaṃ jhāpeti, jhāpenti, jhāpayati, jhāpayanti.

Jhe-ajjhayane saṃpubbo, mahāvuttinā niggahītassa jādeso, sajjhāyati, sajjhāyanti, mantaṃ sajjhāyati.

Te-pālane, tāyati, tāyanti.

The-sadda, saṅghātesu, thāyati.

De-suddhiyaṃ, vodāyati, vodāyanti.

De-soppane, niddāyati, niddāyanti.

Pe-vuddhiyaṃ, appāyati, appāyanti.

Bhe-bhaye, bhāyati, bhāyanti, sabbe bhāyanti maccuno <note>dha. pa. 129</note>, bhāyasi, sace bhāyatha dukkhassa <note>udā. 44</note>, kinnu kho ahaṃ tassa sukhassa bhāyāmi <note>ma. ni. 1.381</note>, nataṃ bhāyāmi āvuso, bhāyāma <note>apa. therī. 2.2.458</note>.

Ṇāpimhi-bhayāpeti, bhāyāpeti, bhāyāpayati.

Īādimhi-mā <pb ed="M" n="0.0403" /> bhāyi, mā soci <note>dī. ni. 2.207</note>, mā cintayi.

Ssatyādimhi-bhāyissati, bhāyissanti.

Le-chedane, tiṇaṃ lāyati, sāliṃ lāyati, lāyanti.

Ve-gatiyaṃ, vāto vāyati, vātā vāyanti.

Ve-tantasantāne, tantaṃ vāyati, vāyanti.

Kamme-vāyīyati, pubbalope vīyati, viyyati.

Ṇāpimhi-cīvaraṃ vāyāpeti <note>pārā. 638</note>, vāyāpenti.

Se-antakriyāyaṃ, osāyati, pariyosāyati, ajjhosāyati.

Kamme-pariyosīyati.

Ṇāpimhi-pariyosāpeti.

§627. **Ṇiṇāpīnaṃ tesu**.

Ṇi, ṇāpīnaṃ lopo hoti tesuṇi, ṇāpīsu paresu.

Bhikkhu attanā vippakataṃ kuṭiṃ parehi pariyosāpeti <note>pārā. 363</note>. Ettha akammakattā dhātussa ‘kuṭi’nti ca ‘parehī’ti ca dve kammāni dvikkhattuṃ pavattehi kāritehi sijjhanti.

Anekassaraedantampi kiñci idha vuccati.

Hare-lajjāyaṃ, harāyati, harāyanti, aṭṭiyāmi harāyāmi <note>saṃ. ni. 1.165</note>, harāyāma, harāyatīti hirī, mahāvuttinā upantassa ittaṃ.

Gile-rujjane, gilāyati, piṭṭhi me āgilāyati <note>cūḷava. 345; dī. ni. 3.300</note>, gilāyanti.

Pale-gatiyaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0404" />, palāyati, palāyanti.

Mile-hāniyaṃ, milāyati, milāyanti.

‘‘Jhānaṃ, ujjhānaṃ, nijjhānaṃ, tāṇaṃ, parittāṇaṃ, vodānaṃ, niddānaṃ, gilāno, palāto, milātanti’’ādīsu yalopo.

Iti bhūvādigaṇe edantadhāturūpaṃ.

Bhūvādigaṇe sarantadhātūnaṃ tyādyantarūpāni niṭṭhitāni.

#### Byañjanantadhātu

#### Avuddhikarūpa

#### Tudādigaṇa

Atha byañjanantadhāturūpāni vuccante. Tāni ca avuddhika, savuddhikavasena duvidhāni honti. Tattha avuddhikāni tāva vuccante.

**Khipa, guha, tuda, disa, pisa, phusa, likha, vadhādi**.

Idha dhātūnaṃ antassaro uccāraṇattho, so rūpavidhāne nappayujjate.

§628. **Tudādīhi ko** <note>ka. 445; rū. 433; nī. 925; caṃ. 1.1.92; pā. 3.1.77</note>.

Tudādīhi kānubandho apaccayo hoti. Kānubandho avuddhidīpanattho.

Khipa-khipane, khipati, pakkhipati, ukkhipati, okkhipati, nikkhipati, vikkhipati, paṭikkhipati, saṃkhipati.

Kamme-khipīyati.

Kārite-khipeti<pb ed="M" n="0.0405" />, khipayati, khipāpeti, khipāpayati, khepeti, khepayati vā, udakaṃ khepeti, taṇhaṃ khepeti, khayāpetīti attho.

Guha-saṃvaraṇe, guhati, nigguhati.

Kamme-guhiyati.

Kārite gussa dīgho, gūheti, gūhayati, gūhāpeti, gūhāpayati.

Kamme-gūhāpīyati.

Ghaṭa-cetāyaṃ, ghaṭati.

Kamme-ghaṭīyati.

Kārite-ghaṭeti, ghaṭayati, ghaṭāpeti, ghaṭāpayati.

Tuda-byadhane, byadhanaṃ vijjhanaṃ, tudati, vitudati.

Assa ette-tudeti, tudenti.

Kamme-tudīyati.

‘Tavaggavaraṇānaṃ ye cavaggabayañā’ti dassa jattaṃ. ‘Vaggalasehi te’ti yassa pubbarūpattaṃ, tujjati.

Kārite-tudeti, tudayati, tudāpeti, tudāpayati.

Disī-uddisane, uddisanaṃ sarūpato kathanaṃ. Uddisati, pātimokkhaṃ uddisanti <note>mahāva. 152</note>, niddisati, niddisanti, apadisati, apadisanti.

Kamme-uddisīyati, uddisīyanti.

Kārite-ācariyo sissaṃ pāḷidhammaṃ uddisāpeti, uddisāpayati, vācetīti attho. Pāṭhesu pana sadvayampi dissati.

Nuda-khipane<pb ed="M" n="0.0406" />, nudati, panudati, vinodeti, paṭivinodeti vā.

Kamme-panudīyati, panujjati.

Kārite-panudeti, panudayati, panudāpeti, panudāpayati.

Pisa-saṃcuṇṇe, pisati.

Kamme-pisīyati.

Kārite-piseti, pisayati, pisāpeti, pisāpayati.

Phusa-samphasse pattiyañca, phusati, phusanti dhīrā nibbānaṃ <note>dha. pa. 23</note>, vajjaṃ naṃ phuseyya <note>pārā. 409; cūḷava. 344</note>.

Kamme-phusīyati.

Kārite-phuseti, phusayati, phusāpeti, phusāpayati.

Likha-lekhane, likhati, sallikhati, vilikhati.

Kārite-likheti, sallikheti, vilikheti.

Vadha-hiṃsāyaṃ, vadhati, vadheti.

Kamme-vadhīyati.

Yamhi dhassa jhattaṃ, yassa pubbarūpaṃ. ‘Catutthadutiyesvesaṃ tatiyapaṭhamā’ti jhassa tatiyajattaṃ, vajjhati, vajjhanti, vajjhare. Ime sattā haññantu vā vajjhantu vā <note>ma. ni. 1.60</note>.

Kārite-vadheti, vadhayati, vadhāpeti, vadhāpayati, sāmiko purisaṃ maggaṃ gameti, gamayati, gamāpeti, gamāpayati iccādīnipi idha vattabbāni.

Iti tudādigaṇo.

#### Savuddhikarūpa

Atha <pb ed="M" n="0.0407" /> savuddhikarūpāni vuccante.

Asa-bhuvi, āsa-nivāse upavesane ca, isu-icchā, kantīsu, kamu-padagamane, kusa-akkose, gamu-gatimhi, jaravayohānimhi, jana-janane, mara-pāṇacāge, yamu-uparame, ruda-assuvimocane kandane ca, ruha-janane, labha-lābhe, vaca, vada-viyattiyaṃ vācāyaṃ, vida-ñāṇe, vasa-nivāse, visapavesane, sada-gatyā’vasāne, hana-hiṃsāyaṃ, haraharaṇe.

Tyādyuppatti, kattari lo, asa-bhuvi, sattāyanti attho.

§629. **Tassa tho** <note>ka. 494; rū. 495, 500; nī. 989, 991</note>.

Atthito parassati, tūnaṃ tassa tho hoti.

‘Pararūpamayakāre byañjane’ti suttena byañjane pare dhātvantassa pararūpattaṃ, ‘catutthadutiyesvesaṃ tatiyapaṭhamā’ti suttena pararūpassa dutiyassa paṭhamattaṃ.

Dhanaṃ me atthi.

Ettha ca ‘‘atthi tvaṃ etarahi, na tvaṃ natthi, atthi ahaṃ etarahi, nāhaṃ natthi, puttā matthi dhanā matthi <note>dha. pa. 62</note>, atthi imasmiṃ kāye kesā’’ti <note>khu. pā. 3.dvitiṃsākāra</note> ādīsu atthisaddo ākhyātapaṭirūpako kattuvācako nipāto.

‘‘Atthīti kho kaccāyana ayameko anto, natthīti dutiyo anto’’ti <note>saṃ. ni. 2.15</note> ca ‘‘atthipaccayo, natthipaccayo’’ti <note>paṭṭhā. 1.1.paccayuddesa</note> ca evamādīsu nāmapaṭirūpako. Tathā natthisaddo.

Tumhi-vipassissa <pb ed="M" n="0.0408" /> ca namatthu <note>dī. ni. 3.287</note>, namo te buddha vīratthu <note>saṃ. ni. 1.90</note>, ettha ca ‘‘dhiratthumaṃ pūtikāya’’nti ādīsu atthusaddo nipāto.

§630. **Ntamānantantiyiyuṃsvādilopo** <note>ka. 494-5; rū. 496; nī. 1019; ‘ntamānānti…’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Nta, māna, anti, antu, iyā, iyuṃsu atthissa ādilopo hoti.

Santi, santu.

§631. **Sihīsvaṭa** <note>ka. 506; rū. 497; nī. 992</note>.

Atthissa aṭa hoti si, hīsu.

Manussosi <note>mahāva. 126</note>, purisosi <note>mahāva. 126</note>. Himhi dīgho, tvaṃ paṇḍito āhi, bhavāhīti attho. Tavibhattīsu dhātvantassa pararūpaṃ, tumhe attha, kaccittha parisuddhā <note>pārā. 233</note>. Tvādimhi-mā pamādattha <note>ma. ni. 1.88, 215</note>, tumhe samaggā attha.

§632. **Mimānaṃ vā mhimhā ca** <note>ka. 492; rū. 499; nī. 987; ‘sīhisvaṭa’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Atthito paresaṃ mi, mānaṃ mhi, mhā honti vā, atthissa ca aṭa hoti.

Ahaṃ pasannomhi, mayaṃ pasannāmha.

Tvādimhi-ahaṃ iminā puññena anāgate paññavā amhi, mayaṃ paññavanto amha.

§633. **Esu sa** <note>ka. 492; rū. 499; nī. 987</note>.

Etesu <pb ed="M" n="0.0409" /> mi, mesu atthissa sassa so hoti. Pararūpanisedhanatthamidaṃ suttaṃ.

Ahaṃ paṇḍito asmi, mayaṃ paṇḍitā asma.

Tvādimhi-ahaṃ anāgate paññavā asmi, mayaṃ paññavanto asma.

Eyyādimhi –

§634. **Atthiteyyādichannaṃ sa su sasi satha saṃsāma** <note>ka. 571, 517; rū. 624, 488; nī. 830, 1105; ‘atthiteyyādicchannaṃ sasusasatha saṃ sāma’ (bahūsu)</note>.

‘Atthī’ti dhātuniddeso ti-kāro, atthito paresaṃ eyyādīnaṃ channaṃ sādayo honti.

Evamassa vacanīyo <note>pārā. 411</note>, evamassu vacanīyā <note>pārā 418</note>, tvaṃ assasi, tumhe assatha, ahaṃ assaṃ, mayaṃ assāma.

Assunipātopi bahuṃ dissati, tayassu dhammā jahitā bhavanti <note>khu. pā. 6.10</note>, kenassu taratī oghaṃ, kenassu tarati aṇṇavaṃ <note>saṃ. ni. 1.246</note>. ‘‘Kiṃsu chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kiṃsu chetvā na socatī’’ti <note>saṃ. ni. 1.71</note> ettha niggahītamhā saṃyogādilopo.

§635. **Ādidvinnamiyāmiyuṃ** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 993; ‘…miyā iyuṃ’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Atthito eyyādīsu ādimhi dvinnaṃ iyā, iyuṃ honti. ‘Ntamānantantiyiyuṃsū…’tiādilopo.

So <pb ed="M" n="0.0410" /> siyā, te siyuṃ, ete dve nipātāpi honti. ‘‘Vedanākkhandho siyā kusalo, siyā akusalo, siyā abyākato’’ti <note>vibha. 152</note> ādīsu ekaccoti attho.

‘‘Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā’’ti <note>paṭṭhā. 1.1.35-38</note> ādīsu kinnūti attho.

‘‘Dvādasākusalā siyu’’nti <note>abhidhammatthasaṅgaha 2</note> ādīsu bhavantīti attho.

Mahāvuttinā eyyuṃ, eyyamiccetesaṃ iyaṃsu, iyaṃ honti, ādilopo, siyaṃsu dve bhikkhū abhidhamme nānāvādā <note>ma. ni. 3.35</note>, evaṃrūpo siyaṃ ahaṃ anāgatamaddhānaṃ, evaṃvedano siyaṃ, evaṃsañño siyaṃ <note>ma. ni. 3.274</note>.

Ajjattanimhi –

§636. **Īādo dīgho** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1001</note>.

Atthissa dīgho hoti īādīsu.

So āsi, te āsuṃ, āsiṃsu, tvaṃ āsi, tumhe āsittha, ahaṃ āsiṃ. Tatrāpāsiṃ evaṃvaṇṇo <note>dī. ni. 1.245; ma. ni. 1.68</note>. Mayaṃ āsimha, āsimhā.

§637. **Aāssādīsu** <note>ka. 507; rū. 501; nī. 1020; caṃ. 5.4.79; pā. 2.4.52</note>.

Aādiparokkhāyañca āādihiyyattaniyañca ssādīsu bhavissanti, kālātipattīsu ca atthissa bhū hoti. Idañca suttaṃ atthissa etāsaṃ vibhattīnampi sādhāraṇakaraṇatthaṃ. Rūpampi bhūrūpameva.

So <pb ed="M" n="0.0411" /> babhūva, te babhūvu, so abhavā, te abhavū, so bhavissati, te bhavissanti, so abhavissā, te abhavissaṃsu iccādi.

§638. **Atyādintesvatthissa bhū** <note>ka. 517; rū. 500; nī. 1020; caṃ. 5.4.79; pā. 2.4.52</note>.

Tyādivajjitesu ntavajjitesu ca paccayesu atthissa bhū hoti. Etena tyādi, tvādi, eyyādi, īādisaṅkhātāsu catūsu vibhattīsu ntapaccaye ca atthissa bhūādeso natthi, sesāsu catūsu vibhattīsu ca ntavajjitesu tabbādīsu ca atthissa bhūādeso labbhatīti veditabbo.

Āsa-upavesane. Guruṃ upāsati, payirupāsati, upāsanti, payirupāsanti.

Kamme-upāsīyati, payirupāsīyati.

Kārite-mātā puttaṃ guruṃ upāseti, payirupāseti, upāsayati, payirupāsayati.

Īādimhi-upāsi, payirupāsi, upāsiṃsu, payirupāsiṃsu, upāsuṃ, payirupāsuṃ.

Āsa-nivāse.

§639. **Gamayamisāsadisānaṃ vā cchaṅa** <note>ka. 476, 522; rū. 442, 476; nī. 957, 1035</note>.

Gamu, yamu, isu, āsa, disānaṃ anto byañjano ṅānubandho ccho hoti vā nta, māna, tyādīsu.

Gacchanto, niyacchanto, icchanto, acchanto, dicchantoti iminā tyādīsu āsassa ccho, acchati, acchanti, so acchi, te acchiṃsu.

Isu-esanāyaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0412" />.

§640. **Lahussupantassa** <note>ka. 485; rū. 434; nī. 975; caṃ. 6.1.105-106 …pe… 7.3.77-78</note>.

Antassa samīpe pavattatīti upanto, byañjanantadhātūnaṃ pubbassaro ‘upanto’ti vuccati, lahubhūtassa upantabhūtassa ca ivaṇṇu’vaṇṇassa e, ovuddhī honti.

Ira-kampane, erati, modati.

Lahussāti kiṃ? Jīvati, dhūpati, ikkhati, sukkhati.

Upantassāti kiṃ? Siñcati, bhuñjati, niggahītāgamena byavahitattā upanto na hoti.

Ivaṇṇuvaṇṇassātvevaṃ? Pacati, vadati.

Iminā issa evuddhi hoti, esati, anvesati, pariyesati.

Adhipubbo isu-āyācane, ajjhesati.

Kamme-esīyati, pariyesīyati, anvesīyati, ajjhesīyati.

Kārite-eseti, esayati, esāpeti, esāpayati.

Isu-icchāyaṃ, cchādeso, icchati, icchanti, sampaṭicchati, sampaṭicchanti.

Kamme-icchīyati.

Kārite-icchāpeti, icchāpayati, sampaṭicchāpeti, sampaṭicchāpayati.

Kamme-icchāpīyati, icchāpayīyati, so icchi, te icchiṃsu, icchissati, icchissanti.

Kamu-vijjhane, gambhīresu ṭhānesu ñāṇaṃ kamati, na satthaṃ kamati, na visaṃ kamati, na aggi kamati <note>a. ni. 8.1</note>, na vijjhatīti attho.

Kamu-padagamane<pb ed="M" n="0.0413" />, pakkamati, apakkamati, upakkamati, vikkamati, abhikkamati, paṭikkamati, atikkamati, saṅkamati, okkamati.

§641. **Nito kamassa** <note>ka. 20; rū. 27; nī. 50</note>.

Nimhā parassa kamassa kassa kho hoti. ‘Ādissā’ti saṅketattā kassāti ñāyati.

Nikkhamati, nikkhamanti.

Kārite –

§642. **Assā ṇānubandhe** <note>ka. 483; rū. 527; nī. 973</note>.

Byañjanantassa dhātussa ādimhi a-kārassa āvuddhi hoti ṇānubandhe paccaye. ‘Bahula’nti adhikatattā ṇāpimhi āvuddhi natthi.

Pakkāmeti, pakkāmayati, nikkhāmeti, nikkhāmayati, nikkhamāpeti, nikkhamāpayati.

Īādimhi mahāvuttinā ādidīgho vā hoti, so pakkami, pakkāmi, idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi, maddī sabbaṅgasobhaṇā <note>jā. 2.22.1857</note>, pakkamuṃ, pakkāmuṃ, sammodamānā pakkāmuṃ, aññamaññaṃ piyaṃ vadā <note>jā. 2.22.1868</note>, pakkamiṃsu, pakkāmiṃsu, pakkamaṃsu, pakkāmaṃsu, pakkamissati, pakkamissanti, pakkamissare.

Āpubbo kusa-akkose, lahupantattā vuddhi, akkosati, akkosanti. Papubbo āmantane, pakkosati, pakkosanti. Vipubbo uccasadde, vikkosati, vikkosanti. Paṭipubbo nīvāraṇe, paṭikkosati, paṭikkosanti.

Īādimhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0414" /> –

§643. **Kusaruhīssacchi** <note>ka. 498; rū. 480; nī. 1114; ‘kusaruhehīssa chi’ (bahūsu)</note>.

Kusato ruhato ca parassa īssa cchi hoti.

Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ <note>dha. pa. 3-4</note>, idañca rūpaṃ kudha, kupadhātūhipi sādhenti, evaṃ sati ‘‘akkocchi me’’ti pāṭho siyā. Akkosi, akkosiṃsu.

Gamu gatimhi, kattari lo, ‘ūlasse’ti lassa ettaṃ, gameti, gamenti. Avapubbo ñāṇe, avagameti, avagamenti, adhipubbo ñāṇe lābhe ca, adhigameti, adhigamenti. Vipubbo vigame, vigameti, vigamenti.

Kamme-gamīyati, gamiyati, gamiyyati.

Pubbarūpatte-gammati, gammanti, adhigammati, adhigammanti, adhigammare, adhigammate, adhigammante, adhigammare.

Kārite vuddhi natthi, gameti, gamayati, gamāpeti, gamāpayati.

Kamme-gamayīyati, gamayīyanti, gamāpīyati, gamāpīyanti.

Hiyyattanimhi-so agamā, gamā, te agamū, gamū, tvaṃ agamo, agama, agami, tumhe agamuttha, ahaṃ agamiṃ, gamiṃ, mayaṃ agamamhā, gamamhā, agamumhā, gamumhā, so agamattha, te agamatthuṃ, tvaṃ agamase, tumhe agamavhaṃ, ahaṃ agamaṃ, mayaṃ agamamhase.

Ajjhattanimhi īādīsu ikārāgamo, so agamī, gamī.

Rassatte-agami, gami.

Mahāvuttinā <pb ed="M" n="0.0415" /> ākārena saha sāgamo, so agamāsi, gāmaṃ agamāsi, nagaraṃ agamāsi.

‘Eyyāthasse’iccādinā īssa ttho, so gāmaṃ agamittho, gamittho, te agamuṃ, gamuṃ.

‘Uṃssiṃsvaṃsū’ti iṃsu, aṃsu, te agamiṃsu, gamiṃsu, agamaṃsu, gamaṃsu, tvaṃ agamo, gamo.

‘Ossa a i ttha ttho’ ‘sī’ti suttāni, tvaṃ agama, gama, agami, gami, agamittha, gamittha, agamittho, gamittho, agamāsi, gamāsi, tumhe agamittha.

‘Mhātthānamuu’iti uttaṃ, tumhe agamuttha, gamuttha, ahaṃ agamiṃ, gamiṃ, agamāsiṃ, gamāsiṃ, mayaṃ agamimhā, gamimhā.

Rassatte-agamimha, gamimha, agamumhā, gamumhā, agamumha, gamumha, agamāsimhā, gamāsimhā, agamāsimha, gamāsimha.

Parachakke-so agamā, gamā.

Rassatte-agama, gama.

‘Eyyāthasse’iccādinā tthatte-so agamittha, gamittha, te agamū, gamū.

Rassatte-agamu, gamu, tvaṃ agamise, gamise, tumhe agamivhaṃ, gamivhaṃ, ahaṃ agama, gama, agamaṃ, gamaṃ vā, agamimhe, gamimhe.

Kamme-agamīyi, agammi, agamīyittho, agammittho, agamīyuṃ, gamīyuṃ, agamīyiṃsu, gamīyiṃsu, agammuṃ, gammuṃ, agammiṃsu, gammiṃsu.

Parachakke-agamīyittha, gamīyittha, agammittha, gammittha.

Kārite-agamāpayi, gamāpayi, agamāpesi, gamāpesi, agamāpayuṃ, gamāpayuṃ, agamāpayiṃsu, gamāpayiṃsu.

§644. **Gamissa** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Āādimhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0416" /> īādimhi ca gamissa massa ā hoti. Saralopo.

So agā, te agū, tvaṃ ago, tumhe aguttha, ahaṃ agaṃ, mayaṃ agumhā.

Īādimhi īsaralopo, agā devāna santike <note>jā. 1.14.205</note>, vāyaso anupariyagā <note>su. ni. 449</note>.

Āpubbo āgamane, anavhito tato āgā <note>jā. 1.5.21</note>, sopā’gā samitiṃ vanaṃ <note>dī. ni. 2.335</note>.

Adhipubbo paṭilābhe, ajjhagā amataṃ santiṃ <note>vi. va. 846</note>, taṇhānaṃ khayamajjhagā <note>dha. pa. 154</note>.

Atipubbo upādhipubbo ca titikkame, nakkhattaṃ paṭimānentaṃ, attho bālaṃ upajjhagā <note>jā. 1.1.49</note>. Khaṇo ve mā upajjhagā.

Etāni o, avacanānaṃ lope sati tumha’mhayogepi labhanti, aguṃ, agiṃsu, agaṃsu. Samantā vijjutā āguṃ <note>jā. 2.22.2264</note>, tepā’guṃsamitiṃ vanaṃ <note>(gavesitabbaṃ)</note>, visesaṃ ajjhagaṃsute <note>dī. ni. 2.354</note>, asesaṃ parinibbanti, asesaṃ dukkhamajjhaguṃ <note>itivu. 93</note>, sabbaṃ dukkhaṃ upajjhaguṃ <note>paṭi. ma. 1.236; ma. ni. 3.271</note>. Ajjhago, ajjhaga, ajjhagi, ajjhaguttha, ajjhagiṃ, ajjhagimhā, ajjhagumhā, agā, āgā, anvagā, ajjhagā, upajjhagā, agū, āgū. Āgū devā yasassino <note>dī. ni. 2.340</note>, cittassa ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū <note>saṃ. ni. 1.61</note>. Cetā haniṃsu vedabbaṃ, sabbe te byasanamajjhagū <note>jā. 1.1.48</note>.

Parokkhāyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0417" /> ādissa dvittaṃ, ‘kavaggahānaṃ cavaggajā’ti pubbassa cavaggo. So jagama, mahāvuttinā upantassa dīgho, kvaci assa ittaṃ, ‘‘rājā dudīpo jagāmi magga’’nti <note>jā. 2.22.911; ‘rājā dudīpopi jagāma saggaṃ’</note> pāḷi. So jagāma, te jagāmu, tvaṃ jagame.

Byañjanādimhi ikārāgamo, tumhe jagamittha, ahaṃ jagamaṃ, mayaṃ jagamimha, so jagamittha, te jagamire, tvaṃ jagamittho, tumhe jagamivho, ahaṃ jagamiṃ, mayaṃ jagamimhe.

Ssatyādimhi-gamissati, gamissanti, gamissare.

Parachakke-so gamissate, te gamissante, gamissare, tvaṃ gamissase, tumhe gamissavhe, ahaṃ gamissaṃ, mayaṃ gamissāmhe.

Ssādimhi-so agamissā, gamissā.

‘Āīūmhāssāssāmhānaṃ vā’ti ssā, ssāmhānaṃ rasso, agamissa, gamissa, te agamissaṃsu, gamissaṃsu, tvaṃ agamisse, gamisse.

‘Eyyāthasse’ iccādinā ssessa attaṃ, tvaṃ agamissa, gamissa, tumhe agamissatha, gamissatha, ahaṃ agamissaṃ, gamissaṃ, mayaṃ agamissāmhā, gamissāmhā, agamissāmha, gamissāmha.

‘Gama vada dānaṃ ghammavajjadajjā’ti sabbavibhattīsu gamissa ghammo, ghammati, ghammanti.

Kamme-ghammīyati, ghammīyanti.

§646. **Labha vasa chida gama bhida rudānaṃ cchaṅa** <note>ka. 481; rū. 524; nī. 966, 968</note>.

§650. **Disassa passadassadasadadakkhā** <note>ka. 471; rū. 483; nī. 951</note>.

§651. **Labhā iṃīnaṃ thaṃthā vā** <note>ka. 497; rū. 477; nī. 1013</note>.

§656. **Āīādīsu harassā**.

§657. **Harassa cāhaṅa sse** <note>‘hāssa cāhaṅa ssena’ (bahūsu)</note>.

§658. **Ādismā sarā** <note>caṃ. 5.1.3; pā. 6.1.2</note>.

Ādibhūtā saramhā paraṃ paṭhamasaddarūpaṃ ekassaraṃ dverūpaṃ hoti, iminā sarapubbānaṃ dhātupadānaṃ padadvitte āsīsa, sīsa iti rūpadvayaṃ bhavati.

§659. **Loponādibyañjanassa** <note>caṃ. 6.2.112; pā. 7.4.60</note>.

Tathā ru-sadde, roruvati, roruvanti.

#### Divādigaṇa

Atha divādigaṇo vuccate.

§663. **Divādīhi yaka** <note>ka. 447; rū. 510; nī. 928; caṃ. 1.1.87; pā. 3.1.69</note>.

Divādīhi kriyatthehi kattari kānubandho yapaccayo hoti.

Dibbati.

Muca-muttiyaṃ, yassa pubbarūpattaṃ, muccati, vimuccati. Akammakattā suddhakammarūpaṃ na labbhati.

Kārite-moceti<pb ed="M" n="0.0442" />, mocayati, mocāpeti, mocāpayati.

Kamme-mocīyati, mocāpīyati, muccatu, dukkhā muccantu.

Ssatyādimhi dhātvantassa kkho, mokkhati, mokkhanti.

Kamme-vivecīyati, vivecāpīyati iccādi.

Yuja-yuttiyaṃ, yujjati, yujjanti.

Kārite-saṃvejeti, saṃvejayati, saṃvejenti, saṃvejayanti iccādi.

Gada-gajjane, megho gajjati, gajjanti.

Pada-gatimhi, uppajjati, uppajjanti, nipajjati, vipajjati, sampajjati, āpajjati, samāpajjati, paṭipajjati.

Kamme-tena āpatti āpajjati, jhānaṃ samāpajjati, maggo paṭipajjati.

Kyamhi parepi yaka hoti, tena āpatti āpajjīyati. Jhānaṃ samāpajjīyati, maggo paṭipajjīyati.

Kārite-uppādeti, uppādayati, nipphādeti, nipphādayati. Sampādeti, sampādayati, āpādeti, āpādayati, paṭipādeti, paṭipādayati, paṭipajjāpeti, paṭipajjāpayati.

Kamme-uppādīyati, nipphādīyati, sampādīyati, āpādīyati, paṭipādīyati.

Uppajjatu<pb ed="M" n="0.0443" />, uppajjantu, uppajjeyya, uppajjeyyuṃ, kinti nu kho saddhivihārikassa patto uppajjiyetha, cīvaraṃ uppajjiyetha, parikkhāro uppajjiyethāti <note>mahāva. 67</note> imāni pana kattu, kammarūpāni.

§664. **Kvaci vikaraṇānaṃ** <note>ka. 517; rū. 488; nī. 1105</note>.

Vikaraṇānaṃ kvaci lopo hoti.

Cakkhuṃ udapādi, ñāṇaṃ udapādi, vijjā udapādi, āloko udapādi <note>saṃ. ni. 5.1081</note> iccādi, uppajjiṃsu, nipajjiṃsu.

Mada-ummāde, majjati, majjanti.

Vida-sattāyaṃ, vijjati, saṃvijjati.

Idha-samiddhiyaṃ, ijjhati, samijjhati.

Kudha-kope, kujjhati, kujjhanti.

Budha-avagamane, bujjhati, sambujjhati.

Paṭipubbo niddakkhaye vikasane ca, paṭibujjhati.
